<script>



  
function getCookie(name) {
    let value = "; " + document.cookie;
    let parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
    if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
}
  
const THIS_API_HOST = 'https://star.thestarmint.com/api/';
// let starModal_cookieValue = starModalLoggedInCustomerId != '' ? starModalLoggedInCustomerId : getCookie('accountId');
let starModal_cookieValue = getCookie('accountId');
let starModal_starIdData;
const starModalCookieName = "starModalHtml-" + starModal_cookieValue;
const allStarsContainer = document.getElementById('all-stars-list');

function setStarModalCookie(objOfHtml) { 
  var date = new Date();
  date.setTime(date.getTime() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
  var expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
  document.cookie = starModalCookieName + "=" + (JSON.stringify(objOfHtml) || "") + expires + "; path=/";
}

  let starModalSelectedProduct;
  let starModalSelectedVariantId;
  let starModalSelectedQuantity = 1;




// document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
//     myStars();
// });

let loading = document.getElementById("modal-star-loading");
let err = document.getElementById("err-message");
async function myStars() {

    // pre-populate modal from cookie if we have it 
    let _storedStarCookie = getCookie(starModalCookieName);
    if (_storedStarCookie && _storedStarCookie.length > 0) {
      _storedStarCookie = JSON.parse(_storedStarCookie);
      let starIds = Object.keys(_storedStarCookie);
      
      if (starIds && starIds.length) {
        allStarsContainer.style.display = "block";
        starIds.forEach(thisStarId => {
          let serializedElement = decodeURIComponent(_storedStarCookie[thisStarId]);
          
          if (serializedElement) {
            let tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
            tempDiv.innerHTML = serializedElement;
            
            // append the first child of the temporary div (which should be your serialized element) to the container
            allStarsContainer.appendChild(tempDiv.firstChild);
          }
        });
      }
    }

    if(starModal_cookieValue == ''){
      return false;
    }
    const CONTACT_ID_API_URL = `${THIS_API_HOST}shopify/customers/getCustomer?accountID=${starModal_cookieValue}`;

    try {
        const responseAccount = await fetch(CONTACT_ID_API_URL);
        if (!responseAccount.ok) {
            throw new Error("Network response was not ok");
            loading.style.display = "none";
            err.innerHTML = "Network response was not ok";
            err.style.display = "block";
        }

        const dataAccount = await responseAccount.json();
        if (!dataAccount?.data) {
            throw new Error("No data in account response");
            loading.style.display = "none";
            err.innerHTML = "No data in account response";
            err.style.display = "block";
        }

        const accountId = dataAccount.data;
        // console.log(`${THIS_API_HOST}salesforce/getMyNFTs?objectID=${accountId}`, ' we doing it ')
        const API_URL = `${THIS_API_HOST}salesforce/getPersonalAndGiftedNFTs?objectID=${accountId}`;
        const starData = await fetchStarsData(API_URL);

      console.log(starData,"starData");
        if(starData){
           await populateModal(starData?.data);
        }else{
           loading.style.display = "none";
          
        }
       return;
        // showModal();
    } catch (error) {
      loading.style.display = "none";
        console.error("Error! - ", error);
      return;
    }
}

  async function fetchStarsData(API_URL) {
      const response = await fetch(API_URL);
    console.log(response,"response")
      if (!response.ok) {
          loading.style.display = "none";
          err.innerHTML = "There is an issue fetching stars at this time. We apologize for any inconvenience.";
          err.style.display = "block";
          // throw new Error("Error fetching stars data");
        return false
  
      }
    
      let responseJson = response.json();
      // loading.style.display = "none";
      return responseJson;
  }

  function showModal(e, variantId, productSlug, quantity) {
      if (e) {
          e.preventDefault();
      }

    if(window.location.pathname.startsWith('/pages/select-a-star')){ // dont run on select a star page
      return false;
    }
  
    // check the url params, not show up if on star detail page
    let url = window.location.href;
    if (url.includes("star-detail")){
      return;
    }
    
  
    myStars();

    starModalSelectedQuantity = Number(quantity);
  
    if(variantId && productSlug){
      starModalSelectedProduct = productSlug;
      starModalSelectedVariantId = variantId;
      document.getElementById("starModal-new-star-url").setAttribute("href", "/pages/select-a-star?product=" + productSlug + "&variantId=" + variantId + "&quantity=" + quantity);
      document.getElementById("product-selected-blurb").style.display = "block";
    }
    console.log(variantId, productSlug, quantity);
      const modal = document.getElementById('starModal');
      modal.style.display = 'block';
  
      const modalBackdrop = document.getElementById('starModalBackdrop');
      modalBackdrop.style.display = 'block';
    
      const span = document.getElementsByClassName("close")[0];
      // span.onclick = function() {
      //     modal.style.display = "none";
      // }
      window.onclick = function(event) {
          if (event.target == modal) {
              modal.style.display = "none";
          }
      }
  }

  async function starModalChooseStar(event, starId, mintedAsNFT, starIsPremium, chartUrl, certificateUrl, starIdentifier, starName, starCoordsRA, starCoordsDEC){
    event.preventDefault();
    // return new Promise(async resolveModalChooseStar, rejectModalChooseStars) => {
    console.log(starId, starModalSelectedProduct, starModalSelectedVariantId, chartUrl);
   
    if(chartUrl && certificateUrl){
      let giftformData = {
          'items': [{
              'id': starModalSelectedVariantId,
              'quantity': starModalSelectedQuantity,
              'properties': {
                    'starName': starName,
                    'starIdentifier': starIdentifier,
                    'starId': starId?.toString(),
                    'starCoordsRA': starCoordsRA,
                    'starCoordsDEC': starCoordsDEC,
                    'chart': chartUrl,
                    'certificate' : certificateUrl,
                }
              }
          ]
      };

      if(mintedAsNFT == '0'){
        giftformData.items.push({
          'id': starIsPremium > 1 ? '46442322821422' : '46442303193390', // star registration default
          'quantity': 1,
          'properties': {
              'starName': starName,
              'starIdentifier': starIdentifier,
              'starId': starId?.toString(),
              'starCoordsRA': starCoordsRA,
              'starCoordsDEC': starCoordsDEC,
              'chart': chartUrl,
              'certificate' : certificateUrl,
          }
        })
      }
  
      let dataAddedToCart = await starModalAddToCart(giftformData, true); 
      if(dataAddedToCart){
        console.log(dataAddedToCart, ' SUCCESS - dataAddedToCart ')
      } else {
        console.log(dataAddedToCart, ' ERROR - dataAddedToCart ')
      }
    } else {
      window.location.href = "/pages/star-detail?id=" + starId;
    }
  }

  async function starModalAddToCart(formData, redirect=false) {
      // document.getElementById("loading").style.display = "block";
      
      return await fetch(window.Shopify.routes.root + 'cart/add.js', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: {
              'Content-Type': 'application/json'
          },
          body: JSON.stringify(formData)
      })
      .then(response => {
          if (!response.ok) {
              throw new Error('Network response was not ok');
          }
          return response.json();
      })
      .then(data => {
          // document.getElementById("loading").style.display = "none";
        
          // If the POST request is successful, change the display of the button
          var btn = document.querySelector('.cust-btn');
          if (btn) {
              btn.style.display = 'block';
          }
          if (window.location.search) {
              const newUrl = window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.host + window.location.pathname;
              window.history.replaceState({}, '', newUrl);
          }
        
        if(redirect){
          window.location.href = "/cart";
        }
  
        console.log(data, 'starModalAddToCart')
        return data;
     
      })
      .catch((error) => {
          console.error('Error:', error);
      });
  }


  function myStarsModal_formatDate(dateString) { 
    const [year, month, day] = dateString.split('-');
    const date = new Date(year, month - 1, day);
    const options = { month: 'long', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' };
    
    
    const formattedDate = date.toLocaleString('en-US', options);
    

    return formattedDate;
  }

  async function populateModal(starData) {
      return new Promise(async (resolvePopulateModal, rejectPopulateModal) => {
        const modal = document.getElementById('starModal');
        // const loading = document.getElementById('loading'); 
    
        if (starData && starData.length > 0) {
            // loading.style.display = "none";
          let newStarModalCookie = {};
            
            
            for(const star of starData){

              // before checkign already loaded star, check the cookie value first

              console.log(star, ' is my star')
              
              
                let findAlreadyLoadedStar = document.querySelectorAll(`[data-starmodal-starid='${star.Id}'] img`);
             
                if (findAlreadyLoadedStar?.length) return true;
    
                let chartUrl, certificateUrl;
                try {
                    const chartResponse = await fetch(`${THIS_API_HOST}chart/create/?ra=${star.Right_Ascension_Hours__c}&dec=${star.Declination_Hours__c}&starName=${star.Current_Common_Name_If_Any__c}`);
                    console.log(`${THIS_API_HOST}chart/create/?ra=${star.Right_Ascension_Hours__c}&dec=${star.Declination_Hours__c}&starName=${star.Current_Common_Name_If_Any__c}`, ' is our url ')
                    if (!chartResponse.ok) throw new Error("Network response was not ok");
                    const chartData = await chartResponse.json();
                    chartUrl = chartData.imageUrl;

                    const originalDate = star.CreatedDate;
                    const parsedDate = new Date(originalDate);
                    const year = parsedDate.getFullYear();
                    const month = String(parsedDate.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0"); // Months are 0-indexed
                    const day = String(parsedDate.getDate()).padStart(2, "0");
                    const formattedDate = `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
              
                    let namingDate = star.Date_of_Dedication__c ? star.Date_of_Dedication__c : formattedDate;
                    namingDate = myStarsModal_formatDate(namingDate);

                    // 2024-03-04 2024-03-04  is the dedication date + naming date right now
                    console.log(star.Date_of_Dedication__c, namingDate, ' is the dedication date + naming date right now ')
                    
    
                    const certResponse = await fetch(`${THIS_API_HOST}certificate/create?starId=${star.Id}&showDate=true&showMessage=true&date=${namingDate}&chart=${chartUrl}`);
                    const certData = await certResponse.json();
                    certificateUrl = certData.imageLink;
    
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error("Error fetching chart & cert:", error);
                }
    
                const starElement = document.createElement('p');
                starElement.className = "star-row";
                
                const aElement = document.createElement('a');
                aElement.href = '#';
                aElement.dataset.starmodalStarid = star.Id;
                aElement.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
  
                    console.log(event, star.Id, star.NFT_Stages__c === 'Requested' ? 0 : 1, star?.premium ?? 0, chartUrl, certificateUrl, star.SIMBAD_Star_Identifier__c, star.Current_Common_Name_If_Any__c, star.Right_Ascension_Degrees__c, star.Declination_Degrees__c, 'clicked star')
                    starModalChooseStar(event, star.Id, star.NFT_Stages__c === 'Requested' ? 0 : 1, star?.premium ?? 0, chartUrl, certificateUrl, star.SIMBAD_Star_Identifier__c, star.Current_Common_Name_If_Any__c, star.Right_Ascension_Degrees__c, star.Declination_Degrees__c);
                });
    
                const imgContainer = document.createElement('div');
                imgContainer.className = 'star-row-img-container';
    
                const imgElement = document.createElement('img');
                imgElement.src = chartUrl;
    
                imgContainer.appendChild(imgElement);
    
                const detailsDiv = document.createElement('div');
                const strongElement = document.createElement('strong');
                strongElement.style.marginRight = "1rem";
                strongElement.textContent = star.Current_Common_Name_If_Any__c;
    
                const spanElement = document.createElement('span');
                spanElement.textContent = star.NFT_Stages__c === 'Requested' ? 'Not Minted' : 'Minted';
                spanElement.style.display = 'inline-block';
                
                spanElement.style.color = 'white';
                spanElement.style.backgroundColor = star.NFT_Stages__c === 'Requested' ? '#6c6161' : 'green';
                spanElement.style.padding = '2px 8px';
                spanElement.style.borderRadius = '5px';
    
                detailsDiv.appendChild(strongElement);
                detailsDiv.appendChild(spanElement);
    
                const extraDetailsDiv = document.createElement('div');
                extraDetailsDiv.className = 'star-row-extra-details';
                extraDetailsDiv.innerHTML = '';
                if(star?.Dedicated_by_Person_Entity_Name__c != star?.Dedicated_to_Person_Entity_Name__c){
                  extraDetailsDiv.innerHTML += "You gifted this star to someone!<br />"
                }
                extraDetailsDiv.innerHTML += `Identifier: ${star.SIMBAD_Star_Identifier__c}<br />
                    Right Ascension: ${star.Right_Ascension_Degrees__c}<br />
                    Declination: ${star.Declination_Degrees__c}`;
    
                detailsDiv.appendChild(extraDetailsDiv);
                aElement.appendChild(imgContainer);
                aElement.appendChild(detailsDiv);
                starElement.appendChild(aElement);

              // PREVIEW MODAL
              let newLinkElement = document.createElement('a');
              
              newLinkElement.href = '';
              newLinkElement.textContent = 'Preview';
              newLinkElement.classList.add("previewLink");
        
              // Attach the showPreviewModal function to its click event
              newLinkElement.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
                  event.preventDefault();  
                  console.log("variantId, id, chartUrl, certificate",starModalSelectedVariantId, star.Id, chartUrl, certificateUrl)
                console.log("star:",star)
                  let target = event.target;
                  if (target) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    showPreviewModal(event, starModalSelectedVariantId, star.Id, chartUrl, certificateUrl ? certificateUrl : "");
                    
                  }
              });
        
              starElement.appendChild( newLinkElement);
              // PREVIEW MODAL END


              
    
                newStarModalCookie[star.Id] = encodeURIComponent(starElement.outerHTML);
                allStarsContainer.appendChild(starElement);
                
            }
            
    
            
            setStarModalCookie(newStarModalCookie);
            loading.style.display = "none";
        } else {
            setStarModalCookie({});
            const noStarElement = document.createElement('p');
            noStarElement.textContent = "No stars found for this account.";
            allStarsContainer.appendChild(noStarElement);
            loading.style.display = "none";
        }
        console.log('Complete populateModal & resolve');
        resolvePopulateModal();
      })
  }

  function hideModal() {
    document.getElementById('starModal').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('starModalBackdrop').style.display = 'none';
  }

  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    document.getElementById('closeModalBtn').addEventListener('click', hideModal);
    document.getElementById('starModalBackdrop').addEventListener('click', hideModal);
  });

  console.log('end of script reached');
</script>

<script>
  


let loading_preview = document.getElementById("modal-preview-loading");
let err_preview = document.getElementById("err-message-preview");
  
async function getPreview(productId, starId, chart, certificate) {

  loading_preview.style.display = "block";
  let modalImagePreview = document.getElementById("modalImagePreview")
  modalImagePreview.style.display = "none";
  modalImagePreview.style.backgroundImage = "none";
  err_preview.style.display = "none";
    
    const previewAPI = `https://star.thestarmint.com/api/productPreview?productId=${productId}&starId=${starId}&chart=${chart}&certificate=${certificate}`;

    try {
        const responseAccount = await fetch(previewAPI);
        if (!responseAccount.ok) {
            throw new Error("Network response was not ok");
            loading_preview.style.display = "none";
            err_preview.innerHTML = "Network response was not ok";
            err_preview.style.display = "block";
        }

        const preview = await responseAccount.json();
        if (!preview.imageURL) {
            throw new Error("Sorry, couldn't get preview.");
            loading_preview.style.display = "none";
            err_preview.innerHTML = "Sorry, couldn't get preview.";
            err_preview.style.display = "block";
            return false;
        }
        loading_preview.style.display = "none";
  
        modalImagePreview.style.backgroundImage = "url('" + preview.imageURL + "')";
        modalImagePreview.style.display = "block";


       
        window.onclick = function(event) {
            if (event.target == modal) {
                modal.style.display = "none";
            }
        }

       return preview.imageURL;
    } catch (error) {
      loading_preview.style.display = "none";
      document.getElementById("modalImagePreview").style.display = "none";
      err_preview.innerHTML = "Sorry, couldn't get preview.";
      err_preview.style.display = "block";
      return;
    }
}

  function scrollToGenerateCertificateContainer(element) {
    let certificateContainer = document.getElementById("certificate-container");
    if(certificateContainer){
      const elementOffset = certificateContainer.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY;
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        window.scrollTo({
          top: elementOffset,
          behavior: 'smooth' // You can change this to 'auto' for an instant scroll
        });
      });
    }
  }



  function showPreviewModal(e, productId, starId, chart, certificate) {
      if (e) {
          e.preventDefault();
      }

    if((productId == '47705286410542' || productId == '48454973522222' || productId == '48454988824878') && (typeof certificate == 'undefined' || !certificate || certificate?.trim()?.length == 0 || certificate == 'null')){
      scrollToGenerateCertificateContainer();
      let generateCertButton = document.getElementById("generate-certificate-button"); 
      if(generateCertButton){
        generateCertButton.click();
      }
      return false;
    }

    const modal = document.getElementById('previewModal');
    modal.style.display = "block";
    
    const modalBackdropPreview = document.getElementById('previewModalBackdrop');
    modalBackdropPreview.style.display = 'block';
    
  
    getPreview(productId, starId, chart, certificate);
            


     window.onclick = function(event) {
          if (typeof modal != 'undefined' && event.target == modal) {
            if(modal){
              modal.style.display = "none";
            }
              
          }
      }
  
  }

 

  function hideModalPreview() {
    document.getElementById('previewModal').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('previewModalBackdrop').style.display = 'none';
  }

  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    document.getElementById('closeModalBtnPreview').addEventListener('click', hideModalPreview);
    document.getElementById('previewModalBackdrop').addEventListener('click', hideModalPreview);
  });

</script>

<div class="chartModalBackdrop" id="chartModalBackdrop"></div>
 <div id="chartModal" class="modal" style="display:none">
    <span class="close" onclick="closeChartModal()">&times;</span>
    <img class="modal-content" id="img01">

<script>

// Open the chart modal
function openChartModal() {

  document.getElementById("chartModalBackdrop").style.display = "block";

  const chartModal = document.getElementById("chartModal");
  const img = document.getElementById("img01");
  img.src = current_star.chart ? current_star.chart : `//thestarmint.com/cdn/shop/t/43/assets/starmint-default-chart.jpg?v=177862634771266987981698323093`;
  chartModal.style.display = "block";

  let isDragging = false;
  let startX, startY, offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0;
  let lastOffsetX = 0, lastOffsetY = 0; 
  let scale = 1;

  function handleStart(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    isDragging = true;
    if (event.touches && event.touches.length === 1) {
      // Use the first touch for single-touch events
      startX = event.touches[0].clientX;
      startY = event.touches[0].clientY;
    }else{
        startX = event.clientX;
        startY = event.clientY;

    }
    startX -= lastOffsetX / scale;
    startY -= lastOffsetY / scale;

  }

  function handleMove(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    if (isDragging) {
    if(event.touches){
      offsetX = event.touches[0].clientX - startX;
      offsetY = event.touches[0].clientY - startY;
    }else{
        offsetX = (event.clientX - startX);
        offsetY = (event.clientY - startY) ;
    }


     updateTransform();
    }
  }

  function handleEnd(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    isDragging = false;
    updateTransform();
                      
    lastOffsetX += offsetX;
    lastOffsetY += offsetY;
    // Reset current offsets
    offsetX = 0;
    offsetY = 0;
  }

  function handleWheel(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    const delta = event.deltaY * -0.01;
    scale = Math.max(0.1, scale + delta);

    lastOffsetX = (lastOffsetX + offsetX) / scale;
    lastOffsetY = (lastOffsetY + offsetY) / scale;
    offsetX = 0;
    offsetY = 0;
    updateTransform();
  }

  function updateTransform() {
    // img.style.transform = `translate(${offsetX}px, ${offsetY}px) scale(${scale})`;
    const totalOffsetX = lastOffsetX + offsetX;
    const totalOffsetY = lastOffsetY + offsetY;
    img.style.transform = `translate(${totalOffsetX}px, ${totalOffsetY}px) scale(${scale})`;
  }

  let touchStartDistance;

  function handleTouchStart(event) {
    const touches = event.touches;
    if (touches.length === 2) {
      touchStartDistance = Math.hypot(
        touches[0].clientX - touches[1].clientX,
        touches[0].clientY - touches[1].clientY
      );
    }
  }

  function handleTouchMove(event) {
    const touches = event.touches;
    if (touches.length === 2) {
      const touchMoveDistance = Math.hypot(
        touches[0].clientX - touches[1].clientX,
        touches[0].clientY - touches[1].clientY
      );

      // Adjust the scale based on the pinch zoom
      scale = Math.max(0.1, scale + (touchMoveDistance - touchStartDistance) * 0.01);
      touchStartDistance = touchMoveDistance;

      updateTransform();
    }
  }

  chartModal.addEventListener("touchstart", handleTouchStart);
  // chartModal.addEventListener("touchmove", handleTouchMove);

  chartModal.addEventListener("mousedown", handleStart);
  chartModal.addEventListener("mousemove", handleMove);
  chartModal.addEventListener("mouseup", handleEnd);
  chartModal.addEventListener("wheel", handleWheel);

  // Remove listeners when modal is closed
  function handleClose() {
    chartModal.style.display = "none";
    img.src = "";
    img.style.transform = "";
    document.getElementById("chartModalBackdrop").style.display = "none";

    // Remove mouse events
    chartModal.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleStart);
    chartModal.removeEventListener("mousemove", handleMove);
    chartModal.removeEventListener("mouseup", handleEnd);
    chartModal.removeEventListener("wheel", handleWheel);

    // Remove touch events for mobile
    chartModal.removeEventListener("touchstart", handleTouchStart);
    // chartModal.removeEventListener("touchmove", handleTouchMove);
    chartModal.removeEventListener("touchend", handleEnd);
    chartModal.removeEventListener("touchcancel", handleEnd);

    chartModal.removeEventListener("click", handleClose);
  }

  // Add click event listener to the modal to close it 
  chartModal.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
    if (event.target === chartModal) {
      handleClose();
    }
  });
  chartModal.addEventListener("touchend", (event) => {
    // Check if the touchend occurred on the modal itself or its children
    if (event.target === chartModal) {
      handleClose();
    }
  });


     document.getElementById('chartModalBackdrop').addEventListener('click', closeChartModal);
     document.getElementById('chartModalBackdrop').addEventListener('touchend', function(event) {

        if (event.target === document.getElementById('chartModalBackdrop')) {
          closeChartModal();
        }
    });
  
}

// Close the chart modal
function closeChartModal() {
  document.getElementById("chartModal").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("chartModalBackdrop").style.display = "none";
  const img = document.getElementById("img01");
  img.src = "";
  img.style.transform = "";
}


 


// Zoom and pan functionality
function showChartModal(event, elementId){
  document.getElementById(elementId).addEventListener("click", openChartModal);
  document.getElementById(elementId).addEventListener("touchstart", openChartModal);

  
}


</script>

    function createShootingStar() {
    const shootingStarMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xFFFFFF, size: 0.1 });
    const tailMaterial = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0xFFFFFF });

    const shootingStarGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
    const tailGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();

    // Initial position of the shooting star
    const initialPosition = new THREE.Vector3(
        Math.random() * 2000 - 1000,
        Math.random() * 2000 - 1000,
        Math.random() * 2000 - 1000
    );

    // Set the initial position of the shooting star
    shootingStarGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute([initialPosition.x, initialPosition.y, initialPosition.z], 3));
    
    const shootingStar = new THREE.Points(shootingStarGeometry, shootingStarMaterial);
    scene.add(shootingStar);

    // Tail setup
    const tailLength = 5; // Number of segments in the tail
    const tailPositions = new Float32Array(tailLength * 3); // 3 vertices per segment
    tailGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(tailPositions, 3));

    const tail = new THREE.Line(tailGeometry, tailMaterial);
    scene.add(tail);

    function animateShootingStar() {
        let positions = tail.geometry.getAttribute('position').array;
        
        // Shift positions back to simulate tail movement
        for (let i = 0; i < positions.length - 3; i++) {
            positions[i] = positions[i + 3];
        }

        // Update the last position to the current position of the shooting star
        positions[positions.length - 3] = shootingStar.position.x;
        positions[positions.length - 2] = shootingStar.position.y;
        positions[positions.length - 1] = shootingStar.position.z;

        tail.geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate = true;

        // Move the shooting star
        shootingStar.position.x += 5; // Adjust these values as needed
        shootingStar.position.y += 5;
        shootingStar.position.z += 5;

        // Condition to remove the shooting star and its tail from the scene
        if (shootingStar.position.x > 2000 || shootingStar.position.y > 2000 || shootingStar.position.z > 2000) {
            scene.remove(shootingStar);
            scene.remove(tail);
            return;
        }

        requestAnimationFrame(animateShootingStar);
    }

    animateShootingStar();
}




        function createStar() {
            const starmetry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, 1, 1); // Adjust the size (0.5) as needed
            const starmat = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0xffffff });
            const star = new THREE.Mesh(starmetry, starmat);
            return star;
        }

        function createStarrySky() {
          for (let i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
              const star = createStar();

          const x = 3000 * Math.random() - 1000;
          const y = 7000 * Math.random() - 1000;
          const z = 1000 * Math.random()
          
              star.position.set(x, y, z);
              starrysky.add(star);
          }
        
      
        }

        // resize
    let thisHeight = window.innerHeight;
    const windowResizeHandlder = () => {
      if (window.innerWidth < 768) {
        if (thisHeight <= window.innerHeight ) {
          renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, thisHeight);
          camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / thisHeight;
        }
      } else {
        renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
      }
      camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
    };

        

        function onPointerMove(event) {

            pointer.x = (event.clientX / window.innerWidth) * 2 - 1;
            pointer.y = - (event.clientY / window.innerHeight) * 2 + 1;

        }



       
    function animate() {
  requestAnimationFrame(animate);
  if (!renderer) return;
  renderer.render(scene, camera);
}



               


   
  </script>
